PS D:\travaux_Unity\PeuImporte> .\verify-scene-setup.ps1                                                                           

============================================
  Scene Setup Verification                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
============================================                                                                                                                                                                                                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
CHECKLIST - Verify in Unity Editor:
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
1. PLAYER SETUP
   [ ] Player GameObject exists in scene                                                                                                                                                                                                            
   [ ] Has CharacterController component
   [ ] Has PlayerController script attached
   [ ] Has PlayerStats script attached
   [ ] Has PlayerHealth script attached (if used)
   [ ] Has Camera component (main camera)
   [ ] Tagged as 'Player'

2. GAME MANAGER
   [ ] GameManager GameObject exists                                                                                                                                                                                                                
   [ ] Has GameManager script attached
   [ ] Set to 'Dont Destroy On Load'

3. INPUT SYSTEM
   [ ] Project Settings > Input System > Active                                                                                                                                                                                                     
   [ ] InputSystem_Actions.inputactions exists
   [ ] Player actions configured (Move, Look, Jump, etc.)

4. UI/HUD
   [ ] Canvas exists in scene                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
   [ ] HUDSystem or UIBarsSystem attached

5. SCENE ASSETS
   [ ] Ground/floor exists (with Collider)                                                                                                                                                                                                          
   [ ] Lighting is set up
   [ ] Camera is not clipping through objects

============================================
  Quick Fix Commands                                                                                                                                                                                                                                
============================================                                                                                                                                                                                                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
In Unity Editor Menu:
  1. Edit > Project Settings > Input System                                                                                                                                                                                                         
     Ensure 'Active Input System' = 'Both' or 'New Input System'

  2. Check Console > Collapse errors (icon top-left)

  3. Try: Edit > Preferences > External Tools
     Generate .csproj files again

============================================
  Common Issues                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
============================================                                                                                                                                                                                                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
ISSUE: Press Play but nothing happens
SOLUTION:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
  - Check if Player has CharacterController
  - Check if camera is child of Player                                                                                                                                                                                                              
  - Press Tab to unlock cursor (may be locked)                                                                                                                                                                                                      
  - Press ESC to show cursor, then click game view                                                                                                                                                                                                  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
ISSUE: Controls don't work
SOLUTION:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
  - Press ESC to unlock cursor
  - Click inside game window to focus                                                                                                                                                                                                               
  - Check Input System is enabled                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
ISSUE: Black screen
SOLUTION:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
  - Check Camera is enabled
  - Check Camera culling mask includes all layers                                                                                                                                                                                                   
  - Check lighting (add directional light)

   [ ] Has CharacterController component
   [ ] Has PlayerController script attached
   [ ] Has PlayerStats script attached
   [ ] Has PlayerHealth script attached (if used)
   [ ] Has Camera component (main camera)
   [ ] Tagged as 'Player'

2. GAME MANAGER
   [ ] GameManager GameObject exists                                                                                                                                                                                                                
   [ ] Has GameManager script attached
   [ ] Set to 'Dont Destroy On Load'

3. INPUT SYSTEM
   [ ] Project Settings > Input System > Active                                                                                                                                                                                                     
   [ ] InputSystem_Actions.inputactions exists
   [ ] Player actions configured (Move, Look, Jump, etc.)

4. UI/HUD
   [ ] Canvas exists in scene                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
   [ ] HUDSystem or UIBarsSystem attached

5. SCENE ASSETS
   [ ] Ground/floor exists (with Collider)                                                                                                                                                                                                          
   [ ] Lighting is set up
   [ ] Camera is not clipping through objects

============================================
  Quick Fix Commands                                                                                                                                                                                                                                
============================================                                                                                                                                                                                                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
In Unity Editor Menu:
  1. Edit > Project Settings > Input System                                                                                                                                                                                                         
     Ensure 'Active Input System' = 'Both' or 'New Input System'

  2. Check Console > Collapse errors (icon top-left)

  3. Try: Edit > Preferences > External Tools
     Generate .csproj files again

============================================
  Common Issues                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
============================================                                                                                                                                                                                                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
ISSUE: Press Play but nothing happens
SOLUTION:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
  - Check if Player has CharacterController
  - Check if camera is child of Player                                                                                                                                                                                                              
  - Press Tab to unlock cursor (may be locked)                                                                                                                                                                                                      
  - Press ESC to show cursor, then click game view                                                                                                                                                                                                  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
ISSUE: Controls don't work
SOLUTION:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
  - Press ESC to unlock cursor
  - Click inside game window to focus                                                                                                                                                                                                               
  - Check Input System is enabled                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    
ISSUE: Black screen
SOLUTION:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
  - Check Camera is enabled
  - Check Camera culling mask includes all layers                                                                                                                                                                                                   
  - Check lighting (add directional light)

// TestStartup.cs
// Simple test to verify scripts load correctly
// Unity 6 compatible - UTF-8 encoding - Unix line endings

using UnityEngine;

namespace Code.Lavos.Core
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Test script - verifies basic Unity functionality
    /// Attach to any GameObject to test if scripts run
    /// </summary>
    public class TestStartup : MonoBehaviour
    {
        void Awake()
        {
            Debug.Log("[TestStartup] Awake() called - Scripts are working!", this);
        }

        void Start()
        {
            Debug.Log($"[TestStartup] Start() called - Unity {Application.unityVersion}", this);
        }

        void Update()
        {
            // Press Space to test input
            if (Input.GetKeyDown(KeyCode.Space))
            {
                Debug.Log("[TestStartup] Space key pressed - Input working!", this);
            }
        }
    }
}
